		<category name="Allegiance Class Mods">
			<category name="Mod Description">
				<comment>By Aaron0000</comment>
				<comment>Modifies most of the Tiny Tina Class Mods and turns them into Allegiance COMs for all manufacturers.</comment>
				<comment>Chaotic Evil Class Mods remain unaltered by this mod.</comment>
				<comment>Class Mods have their own name instead of just "xxxxx Allegiance", along with skin changes.</comment>
				<comment>Designed with vanilla Allegiance relics in mind (though not necessary).</comment>
				<comment>(Credit to SirUmnei for the UI fix as well as a source of inspiration, and Mike for a bit of UI fixing).</comment>
				<comment>NOTES;</comment>
				<comment>If using Sir Umnei's various class mods, load them after this one for them to Sir Umnei's to function properly. Or load mine after if you'd rather have mine override his changes (other than replaced skills).</comment>
				<comment>If using my Class Mods Redux pack, load them before this mod so this mod can overwrite the changes made by Class Mods Redux.</comment>
			</category>
